 Marshal of Indian Airforce Arjan Singh was the first chief in the history of the Indian Airforce to lead the Air Force in any war in the country for the first time
 1 agast 1964 ko arjan singh air marshall kii padavi ke saath chif of air staff banaae gaye
 In 1965, Pakistan carried out Operation Grand Slam against India and Pakistani tanks attacked the city of Akhnoor
 air chif arjan singh kii yah sabase badi chunauti thi

 arjan singh ne raksha mantralay se hamalaa karne ke liye sirf ek ghante kaa samay maanga tha
 As promised, Arjan Singh stood up to his word and made the first airstrike against the Pakistani tank and army heading towards Akhnoor in less than 1 hour

e

 isamen telecom sarvice prowider ke liye paatrata maandand or stock brokaron or anya panjikrut ikaayiyon dwaara anupaalan kiye jane vaale maandand shaamil hai

 SEBI on Tuesday deposited more than Rs 625 crore in a special fund of SEBI in the case of alleged preference (co-location) to some servers of the Exchange, established at a particular place on the National Stock Exchange (NSE)
 Has ordered iske alaava company ke do purv pramukhon par bhi karrwai kii gai he
 The order was given by SEBI after an investigation into allegations of irregularities in high-frequency businesses through the Co-location facility of NSE
 kya hote hai derevative utpaadaiquity bazaar main do segment (hisse) hote hai
 It has a cash segment and a derivatives segment
 ise futures and opshans bhi kaha jaataa he
 Derivative products are securities in which one is an asset or group of assets
 yah asset share, bond, camodity, karency, index future kuch bhi ho saktaa he
 It deals in future, swap, options etc
 sebi ke aadesh main kaha gaya he, 'enesai ko 624
 89 crore and with it the entire amount including the 12 percent annual interest rate from April 1, 2014, will have to be filled in the Investor Protection and Education Fund (IPEF) set up by SEBI
